			W_HR H 0
			"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
			"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
			"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")
			Goto ExpanderLoop
		ExpanderLoop:
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPop")
			loop
		ExpanderPop:	
			"####" "#" 10
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Basic",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
			TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A 1
			Stop
		Death.ExpanderDMGCoop:
		XDeath.ExpanderDMGCoop:
			W_HR H 0
			"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
			"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
			"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")
			Goto ExpanderLoopCoop
		ExpanderLoopCoop:
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPopCoop")
			loop
		ExpanderPopCoop:	
			"####" "#" 10
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Coop",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
			TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A 1
			Stop
	}

Actor WTMWarriorHalberd
{
	PROJECTILE
	+BLOODSPLATTER
    +THRUGHOST
	Species "Enemies"
	Speed 23
	Height 6
	Radius 6
	Damage (random(6,18)/Random(2,1))
    Obituary "%o lost against a Midian Warrior."	
	scale 0.35
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		TNT1 A 0
		W_HX A 0 A_PlaySoundEx("wtwarriors/att1","body",0,0)
	SpawnLoop:	
		W_HX J 4 bright
		loop
	Death:
		W_HX J 1 A_PlaySoundEx("ggen/metal_s","body",0,0)	
		W_HX JJJJJJJJ 36
		stop
	Crash:		
		TNT1 A 1 A_PlaySoundEx("ggen/metal_s","body",0,0)	
		Stop
	XDeath:
		TNT1 A 1 A_PlaySoundEx("ggen/metal_l","body",0,0)
		stop
	}
}

	MeleeRange 80

	DropItem ""
    States {

			W_HR R 0

	}

actor WTRedMidianWarriorSword_Shrink : WTRedMidianWarriorSword
{
	+FRIGHTENED
	+NOTRIGGER
	-SHOOTABLE
	+THRUACTORS
	+NORADIUSDMG
	+VULNERABLE
	+QUICKTORETALIATE
	+COUNTKILL
	-NOGRAVITY
	+NODAMAGE
	+NOPAIN
	MaxStepHeight 0
	MaxDropOffHeight 0
	MeleeRange 16
	Height 16
	Health 1
	Speed 1
	PainChance "ShrinkDMG", 0
	DamageFactor "ShrinkDMG", 0.0
	PainChance "ExpanderDMG", 0
	DamageFactor "ExpanderDMG", 0.0
	States
	{
		Spawn:
			TNT1 A 0
			TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ShrunkToken",1,"SpawnLoop")
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale(scalex*0.2,scaley*0.2) // setting the scale in ACS does work, but the actor shows up at normal size for a split second
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_Shrinker", 0, 1)
			W_HR V 10
			Goto See
		SpawnLoop:
			W_HR R 5 A_Look
			Loop
		See:
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			W_HR R 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly

			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")

			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly

			"####" "#" 2 A_Die("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0
			loop
		Death:
		XDeath:
		Death.Squish:
		XDeath.Squish:
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(64,2)

actor WTRedMidianWarriorSpell_Shrink : WTRedMidianWarriorSpell
{
	+FRIGHTENED
	+NOTRIGGER
	-SHOOTABLE
	+THRUACTORS
	+NORADIUSDMG
	+VULNERABLE
	+QUICKTORETALIATE
	+COUNTKILL
	-NOGRAVITY
	+NODAMAGE
	+NOPAIN
	MaxStepHeight 0
	MaxDropOffHeight 0
	MeleeRange 16
	Height 16
	Health 1
	Speed 1
	PainChance "ShrinkDMG", 0
	DamageFactor "ShrinkDMG", 0.0
	PainChance "ExpanderDMG", 0
	DamageFactor "ExpanderDMG", 0.0
	States
	{
		Spawn:
			TNT1 A 0
			TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ShrunkToken",1,"SpawnLoop")
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale(scalex*0.2,scaley*0.2) // setting the scale in ACS does work, but the actor shows up at normal size for a split second
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_Shrinker", 0, 1)
			W_HS O 10
			Goto See
		SpawnLoop:
			W_HS E 5 A_Look
			Loop
		See:
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			W_HS E 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			W_HS E 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			W_HS F 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			W_HS F 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			W_HS G 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			W_HS G 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			W_HS H 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			W_HS H 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(CallACS("Samsara_Shrinker", 3) == 0, "Forget")
			Loop
		Forget:
			"####" "#" 0 A_ClearTarget

			"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("WTBrownMidianWarriorHalberd_Shrink", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERPOINTERS|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_SETMASTER,0,tid)
			TNT1 A 2
			TNT1 A 0 Thing_Remove(0)
			stop
		Death.ExpanderDMG:
		XDeath.ExpanderDMG:
			W_HQ H 0
			"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
			"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
			"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")
			Goto ExpanderLoop
		ExpanderLoop:
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPop")
			loop
		ExpanderPop:	
			"####" "#" 10
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Basic",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
			TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A 1
			Stop
		Death.ExpanderDMGCoop:
		XDeath.ExpanderDMGCoop:
			W_HQ H 0
			"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
			"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
			"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")
			Goto ExpanderLoopCoop
		ExpanderLoopCoop:
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPopCoop")
			loop
		ExpanderPopCoop:	
			"####" "#" 10
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Coop",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
			TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A 1
			Stop
	}

actor WTBrownMidianWarriorHalberd_Shrink : WTBrownMidianWarriorHalberd
{
	+FRIGHTENED
	+NOTRIGGER
	-SHOOTABLE

	+NORADIUSDMG
	+VULNERABLE
	+QUICKTORETALIATE
	+COUNTKILL

	MaxDropOffHeight 0
	MeleeRange 16
	Height 16

	Speed 1

	DamageFactor "ShrinkDMG", 0.0
	PainChance "ExpanderDMG", 0
	DamageFactor "ExpanderDMG", 0.0
	States
	{
		Spawn:
			TNT1 A 0

			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_Shrinker", 0, 1)
			W_HQ L 10
			Goto See
		SpawnLoop:
			W_HQ H 5 A_Look
			Loop
		See:
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)

			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")

			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")

			W_HQ I 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)

			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			W_HQ J 3 A_Chase("","")

			Goto See
		Grow:
			"####" "#" 4 A_SetScale(0.25*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.25*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.3*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.3*(user_scaley/65536.0))

			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToChildren("ShrunkPropertyTransfer",1)

		Squish:

			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)
			"####" "#" 0 
			"####" "#" 2 A_Die("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0
			loop
		Death:
		XDeath:
		Death.Squish:
		XDeath.Squish:
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(64,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeBootTaunt",1)

			Goto Squish
	}

Actor WTBrownMidianWarriorSword : WTBrownMidianWarriorHalberd {
	Tag "Brown Midian Warrior"
	MeleeRange 80
	Health 60
	DropItem ""
    States {
		Spawn:
			W_HQ R 0
			W_HQ R 1 A_JumpIfInventory("AlreadySpawned",1,"SpawnStandard")
			W_HQ R 1 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("ReMixerSpawnScript",0,1,0)
			W_HQ R 0 A_GiveInventory("AlreadySpawned",1)
		SpawnStandard:
			W_HQ R 5 A_Look
			Loop
		See:
			W_HQ RRSSTTUU 3 A_Chase("Melee","")
			Loop
		Melee:
			TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
			W_HQ NN 2 A_FaceTarget
			W_HQ OO 2 A_FaceTarget
			W_HQ H 0 A_CustomMeleeAttack(Random(20,25),"ggen/metal_l","ggen/swing4")
			W_HQ PPQQ 2
			Goto See
		Pain:
			W_HQ V 4 A_Pain
			W_HQ V 4
			Goto See
		Pain.MightyBoot:
			TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySoundEx("duke/kickhit","body",0,0)
			W_HQ V 2 A_FaceTarget
			TNT1 A 0 A_Recoil(14)
			W_HQ V 16 A_Pain
			Goto See
		Pain.MarathonStun:
			TNT1 A 0 A_Stop
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("NothingSpeed")
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySoundEx("marathon/tech50/stun","body",0,0)
			W_HQ V 5 A_FaceTarget
			TNT1 A 0 A_Gravity
			W_HQ V 30 A_Pain
			W_HQ V 70
			Goto See
		Death:
		XDeath:
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)		
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			W_HQ V 4
			W_HQ W 4 A_Scream
			W_HQ X 4 A_NoBlocking
			W_HQ Y 4
			W_HQ Z 4
			W_HD ABCD 4
			W_HD D -1
			Stop
		Raise:
			W_HD DCBA 5
			W_HQ ZYXWV 5
			Goto See
		Pain.LifeLeech: 
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("SerpentHealth", random(1,2))
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("HealthBonus", 1)
			Goto Pain		
		Pain.Vodoo:
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("Voodoo", 1)
			Goto Pain
		Death.HLLaser:
		Death.HLExplosive:
		Death.HLRPGExplosive:	
			TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfHealthLower(-20,1)
			goto Death
		Death.HLEgon:
		Death.FreemanGibs:
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)  
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("HLGenericGibSpawner",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			TNT1 A 0 A_Fall
			TNT1 A 5 A_FadeOut
			stop
		Pain.Shock:
		Pain.Tesla:
			CBGS M 4 A_Pain
			CBGS M 4
			Goto See
		Death.CalebFire:
		Death.LifeLeech:
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(218, 2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("CalebDMTaunt1", 1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("BloodBurningCorpse_Generic", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_NoBlocking
			TNT1 A 5
			stop
		Death.QuakeElectric:
		Death.NotQuadded:
		Death.QuakeExplosive:
			TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfHealthLower(-50, "XDeathForRanger")
			goto Death
		XDeath.QuakeElectric:
		XDeath.NotQuadded:
		XDeath.QuakeExplosive:
		XDeathForRanger:
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)  
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("QuakeGibSpawner",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR|SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			TNT1 A 0 A_Fall
			TNT1 A 5 A_FadeOut
			Stop
		Death.BittermanDamage:
			TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfHealthLower(-50, "XdeathForBitterman")
			goto Death

			TNT1 A 0 A_Fall

			Stop

			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.95*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.95*(user_scaley/65536.0))

			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)

			"####" "#" 10
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Basic",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)

			TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A 1
			Stop
		Death.ExpanderDMGCoop:
		XDeath.ExpanderDMGCoop:
			W_HQ R 0
			"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
			"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)

			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPopCoop")
			loop
		ExpanderPopCoop:	
			"####" "#" 10
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Coop",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
			TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A 1
			Stop
	}

actor WTBrownMidianWarriorSword_Shrink : WTBrownMidianWarriorSword
{
	+FRIGHTENED
	+NOTRIGGER
	-SHOOTABLE
	+THRUACTORS
	+NORADIUSDMG
	+VULNERABLE
	+QUICKTORETALIATE
	+COUNTKILL
	-NOGRAVITY
	+NODAMAGE
	+NOPAIN
	MaxStepHeight 0
	MaxDropOffHeight 0
	MeleeRange 16
	Height 16
	Health 1

	PainChance "ShrinkDMG", 0
	DamageFactor "ShrinkDMG", 0.0
	PainChance "ExpanderDMG", 0
	DamageFactor "ExpanderDMG", 0.0
	States
	{
		Spawn:
			TNT1 A 0
			TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ShrunkToken",1,"SpawnLoop")
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)

			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_Shrinker", 0, 1)
			W_HQ V 10
			Goto See
		SpawnLoop:
			W_HQ R 5 A_Look
			Loop
		See:
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)

			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			W_HQ R 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)

			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			W_HQ S 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			W_HQ T 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			W_HQ T 3 A_Chase("","")

			"####" "#" 2 A_Die("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0
			loop
		Death:
		XDeath:
		Death.Squish:

			Goto Squish

Actor WTBrownMidianWarriorSpell : WTBrownMidianWarriorHalberd {
	Tag "Brown Midian Warrior"
	Health 70
	DropItem "Witchaven_HalberdMonsterDrop",140,1
    States {
		Spawn:
			W_HD E 0
			W_HD E 1 A_JumpIfInventory("AlreadySpawned",1,"SpawnStandard")
			W_HD E 1 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("ReMixerSpawnScript",0,1,0)
			W_HD E 0 A_GiveInventory("AlreadySpawned",1)
		SpawnStandard:
			W_HD E 5 A_Look
			Loop
		See:
			W_HD EE 3 A_Chase
			W_HD FF 3 A_Chase("Melee","")
			W_HD GG 3 A_Chase
			W_HD HH 3 A_Chase("Melee","")
			Loop
		Missile:
			TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag(NOPAIN,1)		
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("wtwarriors/spells",CHAN_WEAPON)		
			W_HD IJ 5 A_FaceTarget
			W_HD K 2 A_FaceTarget
			W_HD K 2 A_CustomMissile("WTFireMaceBall_Enemy3",25)
			W_HD LMN 5 A_FaceTarget
			TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag(NOPAIN,0)			
			Goto See
		Melee:
			TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
			W_HQ FFGG 2 A_FaceTarget
			W_HQ AABBCCDD 2 A_FaceTarget
			W_HQ E 2 A_CustomMeleeAttack(Random(25,40),"ggen/metal_l","ggen/swing4")
			W_HQ E 2
			Goto See
		Pain:
			W_HD O 4 A_Pain
			W_HD O 4
			Goto See
		Pain.MightyBoot:
			TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySoundEx("duke/kickhit","body",0,0)
			W_HD O 2 A_FaceTarget
			TNT1 A 0 A_Recoil(14)
			W_HD O 16 A_Pain
			Goto See
		Pain.MarathonStun:
			TNT1 A 0 A_Stop
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("NothingSpeed")
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySoundEx("marathon/tech50/stun","body",0,0)
			W_HD O 5 A_FaceTarget
			TNT1 A 0 A_Gravity
			W_HD O 30 A_Pain
			W_HD O 70
			Goto See
		Death:
		XDeath:
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)		
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			W_HD O 4
			W_HD P 4 A_Scream
			W_HQ X 4 A_NoBlocking
			W_HQ Y 4
			W_HQ Z 4
			W_HD ABCD 4
			W_HD D -1
			Stop
		Raise:
			W_HD DCBA 5
			W_HQ ZYX 5
			W_HD PO 5
			Goto See
		Pain.LifeLeech: 
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("SerpentHealth", random(1,2))
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("HealthBonus", 1)
			Goto Pain		
		Pain.Vodoo:
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("Voodoo", 1)
			Goto Pain
		Death.HLLaser:
		Death.HLExplosive:
		Death.HLRPGExplosive:	
			TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfHealthLower(-20,1)
			goto Death
		Death.HLEgon:
		Death.FreemanGibs:
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)  
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("HLGenericGibSpawner",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			TNT1 A 0 A_Fall
			TNT1 A 5 A_FadeOut
			stop
		Pain.Shock:
		Pain.Tesla:
			CBGS M 4 A_Pain
			CBGS M 4
			Goto See
		Death.CalebFire:
		Death.LifeLeech:

Actor WTBlueMidianWarriorHalberd : WTRedMidianWarriorHalberd {
	Tag "Blue Midian Warrior"
    Health 195
	Mass 1000
	Speed 10	
	DropItem "Witchaven_HalberdMonsterDrop",180,1
    States {
		Spawn:
			W_HK H 0
			W_HK H 1 A_JumpIfInventory("AlreadySpawned",1,"SpawnStandard")
			W_HK H 1 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("ReMixerSpawnScript",0,1,0)
			W_HK H 0 A_GiveInventory("AlreadySpawned",1)
		SpawnStandard:
			W_HK H 5 A_Look
			Loop
		See:
			W_HK HH 3 A_Chase
			W_HK II 3 A_Chase("Melee","")
			W_HK JJ 3 A_Chase
			W_HK KK 3 A_Chase("Melee","")
			Loop
		Missile:
			TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag(NOPAIN,1)

actor WTBlueMidianWarriorHalberd_Shrink : WTBlueMidianWarriorHalberd
{
	+FRIGHTENED
	+NOTRIGGER
	-SHOOTABLE
	+THRUACTORS
	+NORADIUSDMG
	+VULNERABLE
	+QUICKTORETALIATE
	+COUNTKILL
	-NOGRAVITY
	+NODAMAGE
	+NOPAIN
	MaxStepHeight 0
	MaxDropOffHeight 0
	MeleeRange 16
	Height 16
	Health 1
	Speed 1
	PainChance "ShrinkDMG", 0
	DamageFactor "ShrinkDMG", 0.0
	PainChance "ExpanderDMG", 0
	DamageFactor "ExpanderDMG", 0.0
	States
	{
		Spawn:
			TNT1 A 0
			TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ShrunkToken",1,"SpawnLoop")
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale(scalex*0.2,scaley*0.2) // setting the scale in ACS does work, but the actor shows up at normal size for a split second
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_Shrinker", 0, 1)
			W_HK L 10
			Goto See
		SpawnLoop:
			W_HK H 5 A_Look
			Loop
		See:
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			W_HK H 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			W_HK H 3 A_Chase("","")

			W_HK I 3 A_Chase("","")

			W_HK J 3 A_Chase("","")

			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)

			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)

			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)

			W_HK K 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(CallACS("Samsara_Shrinker", 3) == 0, "Forget")
			Loop
		Forget:
			"####" "#" 0 A_ClearTarget
			Goto See
		Grow:
			"####" "#" 4 A_SetScale(0.25*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.25*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.3*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.3*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.35*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.35*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.4*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.4*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.45*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.45*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.5*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.5*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.55*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.55*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.6*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.6*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.65*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.65*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.7*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.7*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.75*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.75*(user_scaley/65536.0))

			"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("WTBlueMidianWarriorHalberd", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_TRANSFERPOINTERS|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_SETMASTER,0,tid)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToChildren("ShrunkPropertyTransfer",1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToChildren("ShrunkPropertyTransfer",1)
			TNT1 A 2 Thing_Remove(0)
			stop
		Squish:
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("SquishToken", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeStomp", 1, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)

			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)
			"####" "#" 0 
			"####" "#" 2 A_Die("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0
			loop
		Death:
		XDeath:
		Death.Squish:
		XDeath.Squish:

			stop
		DukeStomp:
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeStomp", 1)
			Goto Squish
	}

			W_HK R 5 A_Look
			Loop
		See:

		Melee:

			W_HK V 4

	}

			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly

		Grow:
			"####" "#" 4 A_SetScale(0.25*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.25*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.3*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.3*(user_scaley/65536.0))

			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)
			"####" "#" 0 
			"####" "#" 2 A_Die("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0
			loop
		Death:
		XDeath:
		Death.Squish:
		XDeath.Squish:

	Tag "Blue Midian Warrior"
	Health 210
	DropItem "Witchaven_HalberdMonsterDrop",180,1
    States {
		Spawn:
			W_HL E 0
			W_HL E 1 A_JumpIfInventory("AlreadySpawned",1,"SpawnStandard")

			W_HL E 0 A_GiveInventory("AlreadySpawned",1)
		SpawnStandard:
			W_HL E 5 A_Look
			Loop
		See:
			W_HL EE 3 A_Chase
			W_HL FF 3 A_Chase("Melee","")

		Missile:

		Melee:

			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)

			loop
		ExpanderPop:	
			"####" "#" 10
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Basic",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
			TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A 1
			Stop
		Death.ExpanderDMGCoop:
		XDeath.ExpanderDMGCoop:
			W_HL E 0
			"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
			"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
			"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")
			Goto ExpanderLoopCoop
		ExpanderLoopCoop:
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPopCoop")
			loop
		ExpanderPopCoop:	
			"####" "#" 10
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Coop",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
			TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A 1
			Stop
	}
}

			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly

			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)

		ExpanderPop:	
			"####" "#" 10

			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
			TNT1 A 0 A_KillMaster
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A 1
			Stop
		Death.ExpanderDMGCoop:
		XDeath.ExpanderDMGCoop:
			W_HG H 0
			"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
			"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)

		See:

		XDeath.ExpanderDMGCoop:

actor WTPurpleMidianWarriorSword_Shrink : WTPurpleMidianWarriorSword
{
	+FRIGHTENED
	+NOTRIGGER
	-SHOOTABLE
	+THRUACTORS
	+NORADIUSDMG
	+VULNERABLE
	+QUICKTORETALIATE
	+COUNTKILL
	-NOGRAVITY
	+NODAMAGE
	+NOPAIN
	MaxStepHeight 0
	MaxDropOffHeight 0
	MeleeRange 16
	Height 16
	Health 1
	Speed 1
	PainChance "ShrinkDMG", 0
	DamageFactor "ShrinkDMG", 0.0
	PainChance "ExpanderDMG", 0
	DamageFactor "ExpanderDMG", 0.0
	States
	{
		Spawn:
			TNT1 A 0
			TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ShrunkToken",1,"SpawnLoop")
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale(scalex*0.2,scaley*0.2) // setting the scale in ACS does work, but the actor shows up at normal size for a split second
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_Shrinker", 0, 1)

			"####" "#" 4 A_SetScale(0.25*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.25*(user_scaley/65536.0))

	}

		See:

			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
			TNT1 A 0 A_KillMaster
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A 1
			Stop
		Death.ExpanderDMGCoop:
		XDeath.ExpanderDMGCoop:
			W_HH E 0
			"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
			"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
			"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")
			Goto ExpanderLoopCoop
		ExpanderLoopCoop:
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPopCoop")
			loop
		ExpanderPopCoop:	
			"####" "#" 10
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Coop",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
			TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
			TNT1 A 0 A_KillMaster
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A 1
			Stop
	}
}

actor WTPurpleMidianWarriorSpell_Shrink : WTPurpleMidianWarriorSpell
{
	+FRIGHTENED
	+NOTRIGGER
	-SHOOTABLE
	+THRUACTORS
	+NORADIUSDMG
	+VULNERABLE
	+QUICKTORETALIATE
	+COUNTKILL
	-NOGRAVITY
	+NODAMAGE
	+NOPAIN
	MaxStepHeight 0
	MaxDropOffHeight 0
	MeleeRange 16
	Height 16
	Health 1
	Speed 1
	PainChance "ShrinkDMG", 0
	DamageFactor "ShrinkDMG", 0.0
	PainChance "ExpanderDMG", 0
	DamageFactor "ExpanderDMG", 0.0
	States
	{
		Spawn:
			TNT1 A 0
			TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ShrunkToken",1,"SpawnLoop")
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale(scalex*0.2,scaley*0.2) // setting the scale in ACS does work, but the actor shows up at normal size for a split second
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_Shrinker", 0, 1)
			W_HH O 10
			Goto See
		SpawnLoop:
			W_HH E 5 A_Look
			Loop
		See:
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			W_HH E 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			W_HH E 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			W_HH F 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			W_HH F 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			W_HH G 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			W_HH G 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			W_HH H 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			W_HH H 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(CallACS("Samsara_Shrinker", 3) == 0, "Forget")
			Loop
		Forget:
			"####" "#" 0 A_ClearTarget
			Goto See
		Grow:
			"####" "#" 4 A_SetScale(0.25*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.25*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.3*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.3*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.35*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.35*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.4*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.4*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.45*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.45*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.5*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.5*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.55*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.55*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.6*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.6*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.65*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.65*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.7*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.7*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.75*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.75*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.8*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.8*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.85*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.85*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.9*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.9*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.95*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.95*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.0*(user_scalex/65536.0),1.0*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("WTPurpleMidianWarriorSpell", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_TRANSFERPOINTERS|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_SETMASTER,0,tid)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToChildren("ShrunkPropertyTransfer",1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToChildren("ShrunkPropertyTransfer",1)
			TNT1 A 2 Thing_Remove(0)
			stop
		Squish:
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("SquishToken", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeStomp", 1, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)
			"####" "#" 2 
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)
			"####" "#" 0 
			"####" "#" 2 A_Die("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0
			loop
		Death:
		XDeath:
		Death.Squish:
		XDeath.Squish:
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(64,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeBootTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/enemygib", CHAN_BODY)
			TNT1 A 1 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeBloodPool",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR|SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("MasterDeadToken", 1, AAPTR_Master)
			stop
		DukeStomp:
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeStomp", 1)
			Goto Squish
	}
}
